 The issue of development was the top word in the speeches of both President Kovind and former President Mukherjee
 mukherjee ne apane bhaashan main 'vikaas' kaa 22 baar istemaal kiya tha vahiin kovind ne 23 baar istemaal kiya

 saal 2014 main mukherjee ke bhaashan main 'vikaas' ke baad infrastracchar (13), technology (11), work (10), investment (10) or policy (10) jaise shabdon kii adhikta rahi thi

 raashtrapati kovind ke bhaashan main jin shabdon ko sabase zyada ahmiyat mili, unamem pramukh hai: suraksha (17), kisaan (15), mahilaayein (14), garib (14), infrastracchar (12), sansthaaen (10), swatantraaa (10), work (10) or arthvyavastha (10)
 Interestingly, the words which are most used in the speech of President Kovind, are the issues related to them in the country at this time
 yani raashtrapati ne apane abhibhaashan main yah aashwaasan diya he ki sarkaar in muddon par gaur karegi
 In the President's speech, the term security has been mentioned 17 times in total in various contexts including internal and external security
 suraksha kaa yah zikr sirf suraksha balon ke sandarbh main nahin aayaa he, balki raashtrapati kovind ne chote vyavsaayiyon ke liye aarthik suraksha or mahila suraksha ke sandarbh main bhi 'suraksha' shabd kaa istemaal kiya he
 The second word after 'security' is 'farmer', which is mentioned most often in the President's speech
 krishi kshetra sankat main he or haalia varshon main puure desh main jagah-jagah kisaanon ke pradarshan dekhne ko mili hai

 raashtrapati ke bhaashan main kisaanon ke baad 'mahilaon' kaa zikr bhi praathamikta main he

 with the little experience i have had, i urge you all to take the time to understand it

 It is not a fight against negative thoughts
